Method: 1) 估计源图的带符号弥散圈(CoC)图与视差图；2) 基于CoC与视差差的线性关系，拟合“源特定光学校准指纹”，将源光学校准迁移到目标焦点与光圈；3) 条件生成式编辑器同时接收源与目标CoC图，执行相对模糊合成，实现按区域的去模糊、保留与再散焦；4) 构建高保真合成数据集（含精确深度、对焦距离与完整EXIF）用于物理监督学习。

Result: 在真实数据基准上，AnyBokeh 在任意到任意散景编辑、从全清到散景渲染以及去散焦模糊任务上取得更忠实、可控的结果，避免了重建全清图与测试时散景级别标定，表现稳定泛化好。

Conclusion: 将源模糊视为可估计与迁移的物理信号而非噪声，结合带符号CoC与视差及生成式相对模糊合成，AnyBokeh 实现了不依赖全清重建的通用散景编辑，并以物理监督与数据集支撑其可靠性与可控性。

Abstract: Depth-of-field control is a fundamental tool in photography, yet post-capture bokeh editing from a single image remains challenging. A practical editor should handle images captured under arbitrary focus and aperture settings. Existing methods typically assume an all-in-focus input, or first recover an all-in-focus image before rendering new bokeh. Such pipelines can discard useful blur cues from the source image and propagate reconstruction artifacts into the final edit. We introduce AnyBokeh, a physics-guided framework for any-to-any bokeh editing. Instead of treating source blur merely as a degradation to be removed, AnyBokeh estimates the source blur state with a signed circle-of-confusion map and a disparity map. By modeling the linear relation between signed circle of confusion and disparity difference, AnyBokeh estimates a source-specific optical fingerprint and transfers the source optical characteristics to the desired focus and aperture setting. A generative editor conditioned on both source and target circle-of-confusion maps then performs relative blur synthesis, enabling spatially adaptive deblurring, preservation, and defocus rendering. To support physically supervised learning, we further construct a high-fidelity synthetic dataset with accurate depth, focus distance, and full EXIF metadata. Experiments on real-world benchmarks show that AnyBokeh achieves faithful and controllable editing across any-to-any bokeh editing, all-in-focus-to-bokeh rendering, and defocus deblurring, while avoiding all-in-focus reconstruction and test-time bokeh-level calibration commonly required by existing approaches. The code and dataset will be available at https://github.com/itsmag11/AnyBokeh.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统基于对极几何的SfM在场景近似平面时退化，难以鲁棒求解位姿。作者将“平面”从限制转为可利用的几何信息源，借此在退化情形（如体育馆等）中提升位姿估计的稳定性与准确性。

Method: 1) 将每个跨视图可见的平面通过单应矩阵分解得到相对位姿候选；2) 以这些候选为边构建位姿图；3) 设计谱嵌入将边依据几何与视觉一致性映射到实数轴，识别并过滤不可靠边；4) 从映射后得分中提取最大一致性的生成树以恢复全局位姿；5) 可利用多个平面聚合，亦可仅依赖单一主导平面。

Abstract: Structure from Motion (SfM) systems traditionally struggle with planar scenes, where standard epipolar geometry-based methods become degenerate. Rather than viewing planar surfaces as a limitation, we propose a unified framework that leverages them as a source of geometric constraints. Our key insight is that each planar surface visible across multiple views provides an independent estimate of relative camera poses through homography decomposition. By aggregating estimates from multiple planes or even from a single dominant plane we achieve robust pose recovery in scenarios where traditional methods fail. We introduce a novel graph-based approach that constructs a pose-graph from homography estimates and employs spectral embedding to identify and filter unreliable edges. Our method maps homography-based pose estimates onto the real line based on their geometric and visual consistency, enabling efficient extraction of a maximally consistent spanning tree for pose recovery. This approach naturally handles both highly planar scenes, such as indoor sports arenas, and general $3$D environments. We demonstrate superior performance on basketball court imagery where existing methods struggle, while matching or exceeding state-of-the-art results on unconstrained outdoor scenes from the IMC Phototourism benchmark.

### [137] [ERA: Entropy-Guided Visual Token Pruning with Rectified Attention for Efficient MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31982)
*Yuhao Wang,Mu Qiao,Haiwen Diao,Yunzhi Zhuge,Pingping Zhang,Xindong Zhang,Lei Zhang,Huchuan Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出ERA：一种无需训练的视觉token剪枝与注意力校正框架，在大幅压缩视觉tokens的同时保持MLLM性能。核心通过熵引导选锚、聚合回收被剪tokens并估计logit偏置，最后对注意力logit注入偏置以纠正“注意力logit塌缩”，在单图/多图/视频和多种MLLM上实现加速且稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: MLLM推理受长视觉token序列拖累，现有训练-free剪枝虽高效但破坏注意力分布，导致注意力logit塌缩，性能明显下降。需要一种既高压缩又不损害注意力与证据保真的方法与统一框架。

Method: ERA包含三模块：1) Dual-view Entropy Pruning（DEP）：从“视觉多样性”和“头级显著性”双视角，用熵度量选择代表性锚token；2) Bias-aware Token Recycling（BTR）：将被剪token回收到对应锚中，形成簇，并估计簇级logit偏置；3) Logit-preserving Attention Rectification（LAR）：将估计的偏置注入注意力logit，纠正剪枝引起的分布变形与塌缩。整体无需训练，面向不同MLLM和场景。

Result: 在单图、跨图、多图与视频等设置以及多种MLLM上，在激进压缩比下仍保持稳健性能，实现实用加速；相较既有训练-free剪枝方法显著缓解注意力塌缩并提升精度。

Conclusion: ERA将“保持logit”的视觉token剪枝确立为高效MLLM的一条原则化路线：以理论支撑、算法设计与可部署实现统一；三组件协同在高压缩下仍保留关键视觉证据并维持模型性能，代码已开源。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) incur prohibitive inference costs due to long visual token sequences. Training-free visual token reduction provides an efficient solution. However, existing methods distort attention distributions, giving rise to a phenomenon we term Attention Logit Collapse. To address this issue, we propose ERA, an Entropy-guided visual token pruning framework with Rectified Attention for efficient MLLMs. Specifically, ERA comprises three crucial components: Dual-view Entropy Pruning (DEP), Bias-aware Token Recycling (BTR), and Logit-preserving Attention Rectification (LAR). First, DEP identifies representative anchor tokens by jointly modeling visual diversity and head-wise saliency. BTR then recycles pruned tokens into their corresponding anchors while estimating a cluster-level logit bias. Building upon this, LAR injects the estimated bias into attention logits, effectively rectifying the collapse induced by token reduction. Together, these components preserve visual evidence even under aggressive compression, enabling robust performance across single-image, multi-image, and video settings on a wide range of MLLMs. Beyond delivering practical acceleration, ERA establishes logit-preserving visual token pruning as a principled framework for efficient MLLMs, unifying theoretical foundation, algorithmic design, and practical deployment. The code is at https://github.com/924973292/ERA.

</details>


### [138] [CoLT: Teaching Multi-Modal Models to Think with Chain of Latent Thoughts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.31986)
*Lianyu Hu,Shengqian Qin,Zeqin Liao,Qing Guo,Liang Wan,Wei Feng,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出CoLT（Chain of Latent Thoughts），用“潜在思维链”替代文本CoT，在多模态推理中以极少步骤实现高效、可监督的隐式推理，显著提速并提升精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 文本CoT在多模态推理中虽然有效，但存在两大瓶颈：1) 生成长文本导致推理极慢；2) 自然语言表达能力有限，难以承载细粒度或高维的推理状态。需要一种既高效又表达力更强的推理表征与训练方式。

Method: 引入潜在思维链框架CoLT：让模型以隐空间向量而非文本执行逐步推理。为避免潜在状态语义崩溃与训练不稳，设计一个轻量外部解码器进行双向步骤级监督：• 前向模式：将当前潜在思维解码成下一步文本推理，以约束语义可解释性；• 反向模式：给定先前文本上下文，令解码器隐藏状态与模型潜在思维对齐，保证一致性。此外加入内部监督，鼓励相邻潜在状态的连贯过渡。推理时移除解码器与内部监督，仅保留少量潜在步骤（可至3步），以获得高效推理。

Result: 在8个基准上，CoLT优于CODI、SIM-CoT等现有潜在推理方法，并超过需要昂贵辅助图像标注的潜在视觉推理方案。相较文本CoT，推理时延降至1/10.1，文本解码时间降至1/22.6。

Conclusion: 潜在思维链在不依赖冗长文本的情况下实现高效、可控的多模态推理训练与推断；通过解码器的前后向监督与内部一致性约束，兼顾语义可解释与稳定性，显著提速并提升性能。

Abstract: Chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning has enabled multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) to tackle complex visual reasoning tasks by generating explicit intermediate reasoning steps in natural language. However, this text-based reasoning paradigm is inherently slow at inference time with even thousands of tokens and fundamentally constrained by the expressiveness of natural language. In this paper, we propose CoLT, (Chain of Latent Thoughts), a novel framework that teaches multi-modal models to reason through a chain of latent thought representations instead of verbose text tokens, which can perform thinking with as few as 3 steps. Naively forcing the model to think with latent states easily produces meaningless semantics and makes training unstable. To effectively regulate the latent reasoning process, we introduce a lightweight external decoder that provides step-level supervision for each latent reasoning step in two complementary directions: a forward mode that decodes latent thoughts into the textual reasoning of the next step, and a backward mode that aligns decoder hidden states with the model's latent thoughts given preceding textual context. We further incorporate internal supervision that encourages coherent step-by-step latent transitions. The decoder and internal supervision are removed during inference to maintain high efficiency of latent reasoning. Extensive experiments on eight benchmarks demonstrate that CoLT not only outperforms existing latent reasoning methods such as CODI and SIM-CoT, but also surpasses latent visual reasoning approaches that rely on auxiliary images with costly annotation requirements. Compared to text CoT methods, CoLT can notably reduce the inference time by 10.1$\times$ and text decoding time by 22.6$\times$. Code is released at https://github.com/hulianyuyy/CoLT.

</details>


### [139] [Automated Background Swapping for Robustness against Spurious Backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32018)
*Cesar Roder,Kajetan Schweighofer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出AutoBackSwap，通过自动前景-背景拆分与重组，削弱模型对背景伪相关的依赖，显著提升含伪相关背景的数据集上的泛化表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度分类器常利用训练集中的伪相关（尤其是图像背景），导致分布外或相关性被破坏时性能崩塌；需要一种无需依赖打破相关性的训练样本、且成本低的方式来减弱此依赖。

Method: 训练一个次级网络进行前景/背景解耦：对少量样本进行patch级标注以监督该网络；用背景补全/填充生成完整背景；再将不同图像的前景与补全的背景进行组合，自动扩充训练集（背景交换+修复）。

Result: 在多种含背景伪相关的图像分类任务中，AutoBackSwap在没有任何“打破伪相关”的训练样本时仍有效，并在一致性的基准上优于以往方法。

Conclusion: 通过自动化的背景交换与数据增强，可显著降低模型对背景伪相关的依赖、提升泛化，且只需少量标注成本，具有实用价值并优于现有方法。

Abstract: Classifiers based on Deep Neural Networks exhibit strong performance across domains, yet can fail catastrophically if they rely on spurious correlations, i.e., features that are predictive of the target label in the training data but are not causally linked and thus fail to generalize. For the vision domain, many such spurious correlations manifest themselves within the background of the image, where only the foreground is predictive of the class label. In this paper, we introduce Automated Background Swapping (AutoBackSwap) to reduce the reliance of classifiers on such spurious backgrounds. AutoBackSwap uses a secondary network to disentangle the foreground and background, followed by infilling to synthesize complete backgrounds, and finally combines different foregrounds and inpainted backgrounds to augment the training data. We find that patch-wise labeling of just a few hundred samples suffices to train the secondary network and automatically augment the full training dataset on challenging image classification tasks. In contrast to many previous methods, AutoBackSwap proves very effective even if there is not a single sample in the training data breaking the spurious correlation. Across a range of image classification tasks with spurious backgrounds, AutoBackSwap consistently outperforms prior methods.

### [140] [Cross-Space Distillation: Teaching One-Step Students with Modern Diffusion Teachers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32020)
*Anh Nguyen,Ngan Nguyen,Duc Vu,Trung Dao,Viet Nguyen,Quan Dao,Kien Nguyen,Chi Tran,Phong Nguyen,Khoi Nguyen,Cuong Pham,Dimitris Metaxas,Vishal M. Patel,Anh Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出“跨空间蒸馏”，用轻量桥接模块把学生模型潜空间映射到教师潜空间，从而在不改学生主干的前提下把大模型（如 SD 3.5、Flux）的能力蒸馏到小模型（如 SD 1.5），显著提升一步扩散生成质量（HPSv3 从 5.4→9.4）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有一步扩散依赖时间步分布蒸馏，但默认教师与学生共享相同潜空间与 VAE，这限制了将高容量新教师的能力迁移到潜分辨率与 VAE 不同的旧/小学生模型；需要突破“同空间”假设以便在不牺牲部署友好的学生架构下获得大幅质量提升。

Method: 提出 Bridge：不改学生主干，构建一个轻量潜空间接口。具体用冻结的学生 VAE 解码器提供空间先验，叠加一个可学习的投影器，将学生潜编码映射到教师潜空间；通过潜域重建损失和注意力一致性（attention fidelity）目标训练，使映射在教师空间中稳定对齐，从而可直接采用教师的分布蒸馏训练学生的一步采样器。

Result: 在多种现代教师模型上，使用 Bridge 的紧凑学生取得显著提升；以 SD 1.5 为例，一步推理保持不变的情况下，HPSv3 指标从 5.4 提升到 9.4，同时维持低延迟与与生态兼容性。

Conclusion: 通过在学生与教师之间加入轻量潜空间接口，可以打破共享潜空间的限制，实现从异构大教师到小学生的一步扩散蒸馏，兼顾质量、速度与部署性。

Abstract: Modern one-step diffusion models achieve impressive quality through distribution-based timestep distillation. Yet, they rely on a critical assumption: Teacher and Student must inhabit the same latent space. This Shared-Space constraint prevents knowledge transfer from modern high-capacity Teachers (e.g., SD 3.5 and Flux) into compact, deployment-friendly Students such as SD 1.5, whose latent resolution and VAE parameterization differ from the Teacher. We formalize this overlooked regime as Cross-Space Distillation, where Teacher and Student differ in both latent resolution and VAE space. To enable distillation under this mismatch, we introduce the Bridge, a lightweight latent interface that maps Student latents into the Teacher space without modifying the Student backbone. Bridge combines a frozen Student VAE decoder as a spatial prior with a compact learnable projector, and is trained with latent reconstruction and attention fidelity objectives for stable Teacher-space alignment. Across diverse modern Teachers, Bridge enables substantial gains for compact one-step Students; for example, it improves SD 1.5 from 5.4 to 9.4 HPSv3 while preserving one-step inference, low latency, and broad ecosystem compatibility. These results show that heterogeneous large Teachers can be distilled into efficient, deployable backbones through a lightweight latent-space interface.

### [141] [FLORA: A deep learning approach to predict forest attributes from heterogeneous LiDAR data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32023)
*Emilie Vautier,Clément Mallet,Cédric Vega*

Main category: cs.CV

Method: 提出FLORA：以八叉树（octree）为骨干提取点云层级特征，并通过后期融合的门控机制整合生态与时空辅助变量；训练单一模型同时覆盖叶展与落叶季数据，比较季节特定与跨季模型；在法国全国NFI 32,052样地上用LiDAR HD数据训练评估六个属性（优势高、总材积、阔叶材积、针叶材积、断面积、株数密度）。

Abstract: Forest attributes are essential for national-scale resource monitoring. Airborne LiDAR metrics are among the auxiliary variables most strongly correlated with forest attributes used in National Forest Inventory (NFI) estimates. However, producing wall-to-wall predictions remains challenging when LiDAR data are acquired under heterogeneous conditions. As national LiDAR programs expand across Europe, variability in sensors, flight parameters, seasons, and scan angles limits the robustness of existing models, which are often calibrated for local conditions. We present FLORA (Forest LiDAR Octree Regression with Auxiliary Data), a deep learning framework that predicts six forest attributes: dominant height, total volume, deciduous volume, coniferous volume, basal area, and stem density from heterogeneous LiDAR point clouds. FLORA combines an octree-based backbone with ecological and spatiotemporal auxiliary variables through a late-fusion gating mechanism. Models are trained and evaluated on 32,052 National Forest Inventory plots across mainland France using data from the French LiDAR HD program. A single model trained on both leaf-on and leaf-off acquisitions outperforms season-specific models and improves cross-season robustness. Auxiliary variables provide modest overall gains but contribute more strongly to species-specific volume prediction. FLORA achieves an rRMSE of about 12.3% (R2 = 0.88) for dominant height and 39% (R2 = 0.74) for total volume, providing a robust baseline for large-scale forest attribute estimation from heterogeneous national LiDAR programs.

*Or Hirschorn,Aaron Olender,Eli Alshan,Ianir Ideses,Lior Fritz,Sagie Benaim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种零样本、无需训练与优化的框架，通过在预训练扩散Transformer中直接注入球面先验，实现高质量360全景图像与视频生成。通过Spherical RoPE与语义畸变CFG，在推理阶段满足ERP拓扑约束，同时继承主流基础模型的创作能力与泛化性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在推理阶段用Spherical RoPE替换标准RoPE：将低频通道重参数化为3D笛卡尔坐标以原生编码球面流形；将高频通道做谐波量化以强制精确周期性，从而满足ERP的南北极与经度环绕约束。再配合Semantic Distortion的无分类器引导（CFG）显式调控几何一致性。方法可直接应用于多种预训练扩散Transformer骨干（Flux.1、Flux.2、LTX-Video），无需训练与额外优化步骤。

Result: 在文本到全景的图像与视频任务上（基于Flux与LTX-Video）取得与或优于需训练/优化的基线的竞争性表现，同时显著降低推理延迟；在多种360生成场景与骨干上表现出良好泛化，视觉质量与几何一致性提升，接缝与周期性错误减少。

Conclusion: 通过在RoPE中注入球面先验并结合几何导向的CFG，可在零样本、无训练与无优化的设定下满足ERP拓扑约束，继承大模型创作能力并高效生成360全景图像与视频；方法通用、可扩展，具备跨模型与模态的广泛适用性。

Abstract: We present a zero-shot, training-free and optimization-free framework for generating 360 panoramic images and videos by directly injecting spherical priors into pre-trained diffusion transformers. Existing methods either rely on costly fine-tuning on scarce panoramic data that limits generalization, or leverage multi-step optimization that incurs prohibitive inference latency. We observe that contemporary generative models natively exhibit some panoramic priors from large-scale training. However, these emergent capabilities are insufficient, as the models fundamentally fail to satisfy the rigorous topological constraints imposed by equirectangular projection (ERP). We introduce a zero-shot and optimization-free approach that resolves these constraints at inference time. Spherical RoPE replaces standard rotary position embeddings: low-frequency channels are re-parameterized as 3D Cartesian coordinates to natively encode the spherical manifold, while high-frequency channels are harmonically quantized to enforce exact periodicity. Coupled with complementary Semantic Distortion classifier-free guidance (CFG) that explicitly steers geometry, we avoid retraining and inherit the full creative breadth of state-of-the-art models. Our approach generalizes across diverse backbones and 360 generation modalities. We demonstrate this across text-to-panorama using Flux.1, Flux.2, and LTX-Video backbones, achieving competitive performance against baselines, all while remaining training-free. ### [143] [PointSplat: Compact Gaussian Splatting via Human-Centric Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32036)
*Yujie Guo,Yudong Jin,Lingteng Qiu,Zehong Shen,Zhen Xu,Jing Zhang,Xianchao Shen,Hujun Bao,Sida Peng,Xiaowei Zhou*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直播/互动应用需要“随取即得”的3D人像重建，但带宽与算力受限。现有前馈多视图方法在视图坐标系中预测3D表示，导致同一主体内容在不同视角被重复编码，产生严重的跨视图冗余，影响传输与实时性。需要一种更紧凑、鲁棒且高保真的3D表示生成方案。

Method: 提出PointSplat：1) 从输入点集估计粗几何代理；2) 通过光线投射裁剪冗余点并建立显式2D–3D对应；3) 设计Point-Image Transformer融合外观与几何特征；4) 一次前向即可直接回归高斯primitive的属性。通过仅在前景ROI内预测，减少高斯数量并提升新视角渲染质量。

Result: 在多数据集上，相比最近的前馈重建方法，PointSplat以更少的高斯和更低的计算/带宽成本实现更高的新视图渲染质量；对视角数量和图像分辨率变化表现出强鲁棒性。

Abstract: Producing 3D human representations from input views on the fly is essential for immersive live streaming systems, where representation compactness is as critical as high fidelity given limited computational power and transmission bandwidth. Although recent feed-forward reconstruction methods achieve impressive quality through the view-centric prediction of 3D representations, they repeatedly encode the same subject content across multiple views, leading to significant inter-view redundancy. Our key insight is to perform predictions directly in 3D space, enabling the network to learn and produce a highly compact representation. To this end, we propose PointSplat, a novel human-centric approach that directly infers Gaussian primitives from an input point set. The proposed method first estimates a coarse geometric proxy and performs ray casting to prune redundant points and establish explicit 2D--3D correspondences. Subsequently, it employs a Point-Image Transformer to fuse appearance and geometry features, predicting Gaussian attributes in a single forward pass. This design restricts predictions to foreground regions of interest, substantially reducing the total number of Gaussians while improving novel-view rendering quality. Extensive experiments demonstrate that PointSplat achieves higher efficiency and quality while exhibiting strong robustness to variations in view count and image resolution across multiple datasets.

### [144] [GEAR: Guided End-to-End AutoRegression for Image Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32039)
*Bin Lin,Zheyuan Liu,Chenguo Lin,Sixiang Chen,Yunyang Ge,Yunlong Lin,Jianwei Zhang,Miles Yang,Zhao Zhong,Liefeng Bo,Li Yuan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出GEAR：通过双分支读出实现VQ tokenizer与AR生成器端到端联合训练，使AR以“可预测性”引导码本分配，显著加速并提升生成质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 两阶段训练（先训练tokenizer再训练生成器）使tokenizer不了解AR生成器的建模偏好，导致索引分布与AR可预测性不匹配；同时VQ索引不可导，直通估计易坍塌，阻碍端到端优化。

Method: 引入GEAR的“双读出”策略：对每个patch的码本分配同时产生硬(one-hot)与软(probabilistic)分支。硬分支供AR做下一token预测；软分支与AR特征做表示对齐损失，仅回传到tokenizer，从而在不破坏AR训练稳定性的前提下，用可导信号引导tokenizer调整索引分布。该框架适用于多类量化器（VQVAE、LFQ、IBQ）。

Result: 在ImageNet上，相比强基线LlamaGen-REPA，gFID收敛速度快至10倍；学到更好的patch级与空间一致特征；方法可推广到文本到图像任务并跨多种量化器有效。

Conclusion: 让AR“牵引”tokenizer，使码本分配更易预测，把对齐负担从tokenizer转移到AR端。与扩散方法强调“语义化潜变量”相反，GEAR在不改变潜变量语义性的前提下提升AR可预测性与训练效率，带来更快更好的生成。

Abstract: Visual generative models are typically trained in two stages. A tokenizer is first trained for reconstruction and then frozen, after which a generator is trained on its discrete indices or continuous latents. This decoupling leaves the tokenizer unaware of what the generator finds easy to model. We present GEAR (Guided End-to-end AutoRegression), which trains a vector-quantized (VQ) tokenizer and an autoregressive (AR) generator jointly and end-to-end, guided by representation alignment. The key obstacle is that the VQ index fed to the AR model is non-differentiable, so gradients cannot reach the tokenizer, and a straight-through estimator collapses. GEAR resolves this with a dual read-out of the codebook assignment. A hard, one-hot branch trains the AR with next-token prediction, while a differentiable soft branch carries a representation-alignment loss that flows back to guide only the tokenizer. The AR model thereby steers its tokenizer toward an index distribution it can predict more easily. This shifts the alignment burden from the tokenizer to the AR: the tokenizer's own features become less DINOv2-like while the AR's become more so, the opposite of diffusion-side recipes that make the latent itself semantic. GEAR speeds up ImageNet gFID convergence by up to 10x relative to the strong LlamaGen-REPA baseline, learns markedly better patch-level and spatially-coherent features, and generalizes across quantizers (VQVAE, LFQ, IBQ) and to text-to-image generation.

### [145] [FaceMoE: Mixture of Experts for Low-Resolution Face Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.32040)
*Kartik Narayan,Vishal M. Patel*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出FaceMoE，将MoE变换器用于低分辨率人脸识别，通过Top‑k路由和多FFN专家实现分辨率感知特征与稀疏激活，在保持预训练知识的同时提升容量，跨11个数据集显著超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LR人脸由于模糊、遮挡、低对比等退化，探测图像可用身份信息少；同时HR图库与LR探针存在域间差异，单一编码器在微调LR数据时泛化差且易灾难性遗忘。需要一种既能做分辨率感知特征提取、又能扩大容量且保留预训练知识的方法。

Method: 在Transformer中引入MoE：将FFN替换为多专家FFN，并用Top‑k路由按token动态分配到专家，形成语义区域（人脸局部）上的专家专精；采用稀疏激活以控制计算量并缓解遗忘；训练时联合人脸识别损失、router z‑loss与负载均衡损失以稳定训练并促使专家专化。

Result: 在11个涵盖HR、混合质量与LR的基准上，FaceMoE显著优于现有方法；在维持或接近HR性能的同时，在LR场景提升明显，且计算开销未随容量线性增长。

Conclusion: MoE可有效用于低分辨率人脸识别：Top‑k路由带来分辨率感知与专家专精，稀疏激活帮助保留预训练知识和提升容量。FaceMoE成为首个将MoE用于LR‑FR的工作并在多基准上取得SOTA。

Abstract: Low-resolution face recognition (LR-FR) remains a challenging task due to poor feature extraction and aggregation, as probe images often contain limited identity information resulting from extreme degradations such as blur, occlusion, and low contrast. Additionally, the domain gap between high-resolution (HR) gallery images and low-resolution (LR) probe images poses a significant challenge. A single feature encoder struggles to generalize effectively across both domains when fine-tuned on an LR dataset, and this issue is further magnified by catastrophic forgetting. To address these challenges, we propose FaceMoE, an effective adaptation of Mixture of Experts (MoE) transfomer architecture for low-resolution face-recognition . Specifically, we introduce multiple specialized feed-forward network (FFN) experts and incorporate a top-k router, which dynamically assigns tokens to appropriate experts. This design emergently promotes specialization across experts for different semantic regions of the face, which enables FaceMoE to perform resolution-aware feature extraction. Moreover, the top-k router facilitates sparse expert activation, enabling the model to preserve pretrained knowledge when finetuned on a LR dataset, while increasing model capacity without proportional computational overhead. FaceMoE is trained with a combined face recognition loss, router z-loss, and load balancing loss to ensure expert specialization and stable training. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first work leveraging MoE for LR-FR. Extensive experiments across eleven datasets, spanning HR, mixed-quality, and LR benchmarks, demonstrate that FaceMoE significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Code: https://github.com/Kartik-3004/FaceMoE

</details>
